```
ì´ ë¶€ì¡±í•´ìš”.
```

**Feature 3: ì„±ì¥ ì¶”ì  ë° ìœ ì‚¬ ì‘í’ˆ ê²€ìƒ‰**

### 4.2 ë°ì´í„° êµ¬ì¡° (Firestore + BigQuery ìŠ¤í‚¤ë§ˆ)

**Firestore Collections**

```typescript
// 1. users (ì‚¬ìš©ì)
interface UserDocument {
  userId: string;                    // UUID, PK
  email: string;                     // ì´ë©”ì¼ (ì¤‘ë³µ ë¶ˆê°€)
  nickname: string;                  // ë‹‰ë„¤ì„ (ìµëª…ì„± ìœ ì§€)
  
  // ê¸°ë³¸ ì •ë³´
  gradeLevel: 'HS_3' | 'REPEATED_1' | 'REPEATED_2+';  // ê³ 3/ì¬ìˆ˜/3ìˆ˜+
  hopefulUniversities: string[];     // ['ê±´êµ­ëŒ€', 'ë™êµ­ëŒ€', ...]
  region: 'seoul' | 'gyeonggi' | 'incheon' | 'other';  // ê±°ì£¼ ì§€ì—­
  joinDate: Timestamp;
  
  // ì„±ì  (ì„ íƒ)
  mockExamScores?: {
    korean: number;      // 1â€“9 ë“±ê¸‰
    english: number;
    math: number;
    art: number;         // ë¯¸ìˆ /ìŒì•…/ì²´ìœ¡ ì„ íƒ ì—¬ë¶€ 1â€“9
    csatPercentile?: number;  // ì „ì²´ ë°±ë¶„ìœ„
  };
  
  // êµ¬ë… ì •ë³´
  plan: 'free' | 'basic' | 'premium';
  subscriptionEndDate?: Timestamp;
  totalAnalyses: number;          // ëˆ„ì  ë¶„ì„ íšŸìˆ˜
  totalChatMessages: number;      // ëˆ„ì  ì±„íŒ… ë©”ì‹œì§€

  updatedAt: Timestamp;
}

// 2. analyses (ì‘í’ˆ ë¶„ì„ ê¸°ë¡)
interface AnalysisDocument {
  analysisId: string;              // UUID, PK
  userId: string;                  // FK to users
  
  // ì—…ë¡œë“œ ì •ë³´
  fileName: string;                // ì›ë³¸ íŒŒì¼ëª…
  imageUrl: string;                // Cloud Storage signed URL (10ë…„)
  uploadDate: Timestamp;
  
  // ë¬¸ì œ ì»¨í…ìŠ¤íŠ¸
  problemTitle: string;            // ì¶œì œ ì£¼ì œ
  problemDescription: string;      // ìƒì„¸ ì„¤ëª…
  prepTime: number;                // ì†Œìš” ì‹œê°„ (ë¶„)
  isExamSimulation: boolean;        // ì‹œí—˜ í˜„ì¥ ì‹œë®¬ë ˆì´ì…˜ ì—¬ë¶€
  
  // Vision ë¶„ì„ ê²°ê³¼ (LLM ì‘ë‹µ, snake_case ì €ì¥)
  analysisResult: {
    density_score: number;           // 0â€“100, ë°€ë„
    shape_power_score: number;       // í˜•íƒœë ¥
    completion_score: number;        // ì™„ì„±ë„
    coherence_score: number;         // ì •í•©ì„± (ë¬¸ì œ ì´í•´)
    thinking_power_score: number;    // ì‚¬ê³ ë ¥
    
    density_analysis: string;        // ìƒì„¸ ì„¤ëª… (ë¬¸ë‹¨)
    shape_power_analysis: string;
    completion_analysis: string;
    coherence_analysis: string;
    thinking_power_analysis: string;

    color_palette: string[];         // ['#FF5733', '#3DB8FF', ...]
    keywords: string[];              // ['ë¯¸ë‹ˆë©€', 'í†¤ ì°¨ë¶„', ...]
    
    overall_score: number;           // ê°€ì¤‘ í‰ê·  (0â€“100)
    grade: 'S' | 'A+' | 'A' | 'A-' | 'B' | 'B-' | 'C';
    percentile: number;              // ìƒìœ„ ëª‡ % (0â€“100)
  };
  
  // Diagnosis (ê·œì¹™ ê¸°ë°˜ í›„ì²˜ë¦¬)
  diagnosis: {
    fixScope: 'StructureRebuild' | 'DetailTuning';
    strengths: string[];             // ê°•ì  3ê°œ
    weaknesses: string[];            // ì•½ì  3ê°œ
    nextActions: ActionItem[];       // ë‹¤ìŒ ê³¼ì œ 5â€“7ê°œ
    recommendedFocusWeeks: number;   // ì§‘ì¤‘ ê¶Œì¥ ê¸°ê°„ (ì£¼)
  };
  
  // ì„ë² ë”©
  imageEmbedding: number[];          // 1408-dim vector (multimodalembedding@001)
  
  // ì…ì‹œ ì˜ˆì¸¡
  universityPredictions: {
    university: string;              // 'ê±´êµ­ëŒ€', 'ë™êµ­ëŒ€', ...
    major: string;                   // 'ë””ìì¸í•™ê³¼', 'ì‹œê°ë””ìì¸', ...
    admissionType: 'practical' | 'portfolio';
    line: 'TOP' | 'HIGH' | 'MID' | 'LOW';
    estimatedProbability: number;    // í•©ê²© í™•ë¥  (0â€“1)
    reasoning: string;               // "í˜„ì¬ ì‹¤ê¸° ì ìˆ˜ 75 + ì„±ì  1ë“±ê¸‰ â†’ ..."
  }[];
  
  // ë©”íƒ€ë°ì´í„°
  analysisTime: number;             // ì´ ì†Œìš” ì‹œê°„ (ì´ˆ)
  engineVersion: string;            // 'v3.0'
  createdAt: Timestamp;
}

interface ActionItem {
  order: number;
  title: string;                   // "ë§ˆê° ì—°ìŠµ (1ì£¼)"
  description: string;
  durationWeeks: number;
  dailyMinutes: number;            // í•˜ë£¨ ê¶Œì¥ ì‹œê°„
  expectedImprovement: {
    metric: 'density' | 'shape_power' | 'completion' | 'coherence' | 'thinking_power';
    estimatedIncrease: number;      // ì˜ˆ: +10 (ì ìˆ˜ 10 ìƒí–¥ ì˜ˆìƒ)
  };
}

// 3. chatSessions (ì±„íŒ… ì„¸ì…˜)
interface ChatSessionDocument {
  sessionId: string;               // UUID, PK
  userId: string;                  // FK to users
  analysisId: string;              // FK to analyses (ì–´ëŠ ì‘í’ˆ ë¶„ì„ ê¸°ë°˜)
  
  fixScope: 'StructureRebuild' | 'DetailTuning';  // ì´ ì„¸ì…˜ì˜ fixScope

  messageCount: number;
  
  createdAt: Timestamp;
  updatedAt: Timestamp;
  expiresAt: Timestamp;            // 1ë‹¬ í›„ ìë™ ì‚­ì œ
}

interface ChatMessage {
  role: 'user' | 'assistant';

  tokensUsed?: number;             // ë¹„ìš© ì¶”ì ìš©
}

// 4. universityDatabase (ì…ì‹œ ì°¸ê³  ë°ì´í„°)
interface UniversityDatabaseRecord {
  recordId: string;
  university: string;
  major: string;
  admissionType: 'practical' | 'portfolio';
  year: number;                    // ì…ì‹œ ì—°ë„ (2024, 2025, ...)
  
  // í•©ê²©ì ë¶„ì„
  passingCount: number;
  competitiveRange: {
    minScore: number;              // ì´ ìˆ˜ì¤€ ì´ìƒì´ í•©ê²©
    avgScore: number;
    maxScore: number;
  };
  
  // ì‹¤ì œ í‰ê°€ ë©”íŠ¸ë¦­ (ì›ì¥ í‰ê°€ ê¸°ë°˜, 1ì°¨ PRD NeoPrime)
  avgDensity?: number;
  avgShapePower?: number;
  avgCompletion?: number;
  
  createdAt: Timestamp;
}

// 5. feedbackTemplates (AI ë©˜í†  í”¼ë“œë°± í…œí”Œë¦¿)
interface FeedbackTemplate {
  templateId: string;

  metric: 'density' | 'shape_power' | 'completion' | 'coherence' | 'thinking_power';
  scoreRange: [number, number];    // ì˜ˆ: [50, 60]
  
  feedbackTemplate: string;        // "{metric} ì ìˆ˜ê°€ {score}ë¡œ ë¶€ì¡±í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤. ..."
  actionItems: ActionItem[];
  
  version: number;                 // A/B í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ë° ë²„ì „ ê´€ë¦¬
  createdAt: Timestamp;
}
```

**BigQuery Tables**

```sql
-- 1. bq_analyses_history (Firestore analyses ì˜ ì½ê¸° ë³µì œë³¸)
CREATE TABLE `{project}.designmate.analyses_history` (
  analysisId STRING NOT NULL,
  userId STRING NOT NULL,
  uploadDate TIMESTAMP,
  
  -- 5ê°œ ì§€í‘œ (floats)
  density_score FLOAT64,
  shape_power_score FLOAT64,
  completion_score FLOAT64,
  coherence_score FLOAT64,
  thinking_power_score FLOAT64,
  overall_score FLOAT64,
  
  -- ì§„ë‹¨
  fixScope STRING,           -- 'StructureRebuild', 'DetailTuning'
  
  -- ì˜ˆì¸¡
  topUniversity STRING,      -- ê°€ì¥ ë†’ì€ í•©ê²© í™•ë¥  ëŒ€í•™
  topLine STRING,            -- 'TOP', 'HIGH', 'MID', 'LOW'
  topProbability FLOAT64,
  
  gradeLevel STRING,         -- ì‚¬ìš©ì ì •ë³´
  region STRING,
  
  -- ì¸ë±ìŠ¤ìš©
  createdDate DATE,
  createdAt TIMESTAMP,
  
  PRIMARY KEY (analysisId) NOT ENFORCED
);

-- 2. bq_university_analysis (ì…ì‹œ DB í†µê³„)
CREATE TABLE `{project}.designmate.university_analysis` (
  university STRING NOT NULL,
  major STRING NOT NULL,
  admissionType STRING,           -- 'practical', 'portfolio'
  year INT64,
  
  -- í•©ê²©ì í†µê³„
  passingCount INT64,
  avgOverallScore FLOAT64,
  avgDensity FLOAT64,
  avgShapePower FLOAT64,
  avgCompletion FLOAT64,
  avgCoherence FLOAT64,
  avgThinkingPower FLOAT64,
  
  percentile_75 FLOAT64,          -- ìƒìœ„ 25% ì»¤íŠ¸ë¼ì¸
  percentile_50 FLOAT64,          -- ì¤‘ì•™ê°’
  
  PRIMARY KEY (university, major, year) NOT ENFORCED
);

-- 3. bq_user_growth (ì‚¬ìš©ì ì„±ì¥ ë¶„ì„)
CREATE TABLE `{project}.designmate.user_growth` (
  userId STRING NOT NULL,
  analysisCount INT64,
  
  -- ì„±ì¥ ì¶”ì„¸
  firstAnalysisDate DATE,
  lastAnalysisDate DATE,
  daysActive INT64,
  
  -- í‰ê·  ì ìˆ˜ ì¶”ì´
  avgScoreWeek1 FLOAT64,
  avgScoreWeek2 FLOAT64,
  avgScoreWeek4 FLOAT64,
  avgScoreLatest FLOAT64,
  
  -- ë¼ì¸ ë³€í™”
  initialLine STRING,
  latestLine STRING,            -- 'TOP', 'HIGH', 'MID', 'LOW'
  
  -- êµ¬ë… ì •ë³´
  plan STRING,
  paidDays INT64,
  churnRisk BOOL,               -- ì¶”ì¸¡ ì´íƒˆ ìœ„í—˜
  
  createdAt TIMESTAMP,
  updatedAt TIMESTAMP
);

-- 4. bq_ai_cost_tracking (AI API ë¹„ìš© ì¶”ì )
CREATE TABLE `{project}.designmate.ai_cost_tracking` (
  trackingId STRING NOT NULL,
  userId STRING NOT NULL,
  analysisId STRING,
  sessionId STRING,
  
  service STRING,               -- 'gemini-vision', 'gemini-chat', 'embedding'
  model STRING,                 -- 'gemini-3-pro-preview', 'gemini-2.5-flash', 'multimodalembedding@001'
  inputTokens INT64,
  outputTokens INT64,
  
  costUsd FLOAT64,              -- ì˜ˆìƒ ë¹„ìš©
  
  createdAt TIMESTAMP
);
```

### 4.3 ê¸°ìˆ  ì•„í‚¤í…ì²˜

**System Architecture**

```
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚                     FRONTEND (Web/App)                           â”‚
â”‚  - Next.js 14 (React 19) + TypeScript                            â”‚
â”‚  - Tailwind CSS + Shadcn/ui                                      â”‚
â”‚  - Firebase SDK (Auth, Firestore real-time)                     â”‚
â”‚  - Zustand (ìƒíƒœ ê´€ë¦¬)                                            â”‚
```

```typescript
 * 
 * @return {
 *   success: boolean,
 *   analysisId: string,
 *   analysis: AnalysisDocument,
 *   universityPredictions: UniversityPrediction[],
 *   estimatedTime: number (ì´ˆ),
 *   nextSteps: string[]
 * }
 */
exports.analyzeDesign = onCall<AnalyzeDesignRequest, AnalyzeDesignResponse>(
  { timeoutSeconds: 300, memory: "512MB", region: "asia-northeast3" },
  async (request) => {
    const { imageData, mimeType, problemText, prepTime, isExamSimulation } = request.data;
    
    try {
      // 1. Storage ì—…ë¡œë“œ
      const imageUrl = await uploadToStorage(imageData, mimeType, request.auth.uid);
      
      // 2. Vision ë¶„ì„
      const analysisResult = await analyzeWithVision(imageUrl, problemText);
      
      // 3. fixScope ê³„ì‚°
      const diagnosis = computeFixScope(analysisResult);
      
      // 4. Embedding ìƒì„±
      const embedding = await generateEmbedding(imageUrl);
      
      // 5. ì…ì‹œ ì˜ˆì¸¡
      const predictions = await computeUniversityPredictions(
        request.auth.uid,
        analysisResult
      );
      
      // 6. Firestore ì €ì¥
      const analysisId = await saveAnalysis({
        userId: request.auth.uid,
        analysisResult,
        diagnosis,
        embedding,
        predictions,
        imageUrl,
        problemText,
        prepTime,
        isExamSimulation
      });
      
      // 7. BigQuery ë¡œê¹… (ë¹„ë™ê¸°)
      logToBigQuery({ analysisId, userId: request.auth.uid, ...analysisResult });
      
      return {
        success: true,
        analysisId,
        analysis: analysisResult,
        universityPredictions: predictions,
        nextSteps: diagnosis.nextActions
      };
    } catch (error) {
      return { success: false, error: error.message };
    }
  }
);
```

**Function 2: chatWithMentor**

```typescript
/**
 * AI ë””ìì¸ ë©˜í†  ì±„íŒ…
 * 
 * @param req.sessionId: string (ê¸°ì¡´) or null (ì‹ ê·œ)
 * @param req.analysisId: string
 * @param req.userMessage: string
 * @param req.fixScope: 'StructureRebuild' | 'DetailTuning'
 * 
 * @return {
 *   sessionId: string,
 *   response: string,
 *   tokensUsed: number,
 *   nextRecommendation?: string
 * }
 */
exports.chatWithMentor = onCall<ChatWithMentorRequest, ChatWithMentorResponse>(
  { timeoutSeconds: 120, memory: "256MB", region: "asia-northeast3" },
  async (request) => {
    const { sessionId, analysisId, userMessage, fixScope } = request.data;
    
    try {
      // 1. ë¶„ì„ ê²°ê³¼ ë¡œë“œ
      const analysis = await getAnalysis(analysisId);
      
      // 2. fixScopeì— ë§ì¶˜ System Prompt ì„ íƒ
      const systemPrompt = fixScope === 'StructureRebuild' 
        ? STRUCTURE_REBUILD_PROMPT 
        : DETAIL_TUNING_PROMPT;
      
      // 3. Chat íˆìŠ¤í† ë¦¬ ë¡œë“œ (ê¸°ì¡´ ì„¸ì…˜)
      let chatHistory = [];
      if (sessionId) {
        chatHistory = await getChatHistory(sessionId);
      }
      
      // 4. Gemini Chat í˜¸ì¶œ
      const response = await chatWithGemini({
        systemPrompt,
        messages: [...chatHistory, { role: 'user', content: userMessage }],
        analysisContext: analysis,
        temperature: 0.7
      });
      
      // 5. ì„¸ì…˜ ì €ì¥ ë˜ëŠ” ì—…ë°ì´íŠ¸
      const newSessionId = await saveChatSession({
        sessionId,
        userId: request.auth.uid,
        analysisId,
        fixScope,
        message: { role: 'user', content: userMessage },
        response: response.text
      });
      
      return {
        sessionId: newSessionId,
        response: response.text,
        tokensUsed: response.tokensUsed
      };
    } catch (error) {
      return { success: false, error: error.message };
    }
  }
);
```

**Function 3: searchSimilar**

```typescript
/**
 * ë²¡í„° ê¸°ë°˜ ìœ ì‚¬ ì‘í’ˆ ê²€ìƒ‰
 * 
 * @param req.analysisId: string
 * @param req.topK: number (ê¸°ë³¸ê°’: 10)
 * @param req.minSimilarity: number (0.7 ê¸°ë³¸ê°’)
 * 
 * @return {
 *   similarAnalyses: {
 *     analysisId: string,
 *     university: string,
 *     admissionYear: number,
 *     passedFlag: boolean,
 *     similarity: number (COSINE, 0-1),
 *     scores: { density, shapepower, ... },
 *     comparison: string (ë‹¹ì‹ ê³¼ì˜ ì°¨ì´ì )
 *   }[]
 * }
 */
exports.searchSimilar = onCall<SearchSimilarRequest, SearchSimilarResponse>(
  { timeoutSeconds: 60, memory: "512MB", region: "asia-northeast3" },
  async (request) => {
    const { analysisId, topK = 10, minSimilarity = 0.7 } = request.data;
    
    try {
      // 1. í˜„ì¬ ë¶„ì„ì˜ embedding ë¡œë“œ
      const currentAnalysis = await getAnalysis(analysisId);
      const currentEmbedding = currentAnalysis.imageEmbedding;
      
      // 2. Firestore Vector Search
      const similarDocs = await queryVectorSearch({
        collection: 'analyses',
        vectorField: 'imageEmbedding',
        queryVector: currentEmbedding,
        distance: 'COSINE',
        topK,
        minSimilarity
      });
      
      // 3. BigQuery ì¡°ì¸ (ì…ì‹œ ì •ë³´)
      const enrichedResults = await enrichWithUniversityData(similarDocs);
      
      // 4. ë¹„êµ ë¶„ì„ ìƒì„± (LLM)
      const comparisons = await generateComparisons(currentAnalysis, enrichedResults);
      
      return {
        similarAnalyses: comparisons,
        totalFound: comparisons.length,
        queryVector: currentEmbedding  // ë””ë²„ê¹…ìš©
      };
    } catch (error) {
      return { success: false, error: error.message };
    }
  }
);
```

## 7. Competitive Advantage: ê²½ìŸ ìš°ìœ„

### 7.1 í•µì‹¬ ì°¨ë³„í™” í¬ì¸íŠ¸

| ê´€ì  | ê²½ìŸì‚¬ | DesignMate |
|------|--------|-----------|
| **ë°ì´í„°** | 0ì—ì„œ ìˆ˜ì§‘ ì‹œì‘ | **226,695í–‰ ì…ì‹œ DB ì¦‰ì‹œ í™œìš©** (NeoPrime) |
| **ì‹¤ê¸° í‰ê°€** | ì—†ìŒ ë˜ëŠ” ì£¼ê´€ì  | **Vision AI ì •ëŸ‰í™”** (0-100ì , 5ê°œ ì§€í‘œ) |
| **ì…ì‹œ í†µí•©** | ì„±ì ë§Œ ë˜ëŠ” ì‹¤ê¸°ë§Œ | **ì„±ì  + ì‹¤ê¸° í†µí•© ì˜ˆì¸¡** |
| **í”¼ë“œë°±** | ì¶”ìƒì  ë˜ëŠ” ì—†ìŒ | **fixScope ìš°ì„ ìˆœìœ„í™” + êµ¬ì²´ì  ì•¡ì…˜** |
| **ê°€ê²©** | ì›” 50-150ë§Œì› (í•™ì›) | **ì›” 2-5ë§Œì›** (97% ì €ë ´) |
| **ì ‘ê·¼ì„±** | ì˜¤í”„ë¼ì¸, ì§€ì—­ í¸ì°¨ | **ì˜¨ë¼ì¸ 24/7, ì „êµ­** |

### 7.2 Moat (ì§„ì…ì¥ë²½)

**Moat 1: Vision AI + ì…ì‹œ DB ê²°í•© (ê¸°ìˆ ì )**
- **dysapp 3-Layer í”„ë ˆì„** + **NeoPrime ì…ì‹œ ë°ì´í„°** í†µí•©
- ë‹¨ìˆœ AI í‰ê°€ê°€ ì•„ë‹Œ, "ì…ì‹œ í†µê³„ ê¸°ë°˜ ë¼ì¸ ì¶”ì •"
- ê²½ìŸì‚¬ê°€ ë”°ë¼í•˜ë ¤ë©´:
  1. Vision AI ëª¨ë¸ í›ˆë ¨ (6ê°œì›”+)
  2. ì…ì‹œ ë°ì´í„° ìˆ˜ì§‘ (2ë…„+)
  3. ë‘ ë°ì´í„°ì˜ ìƒê´€ê´€ê³„ ëª¨ë¸ë§ (6ê°œì›”+)
  - **ì´ 3ë…„ ì´ìƒ ì†Œìš”** â†’ ê°•ë ¥í•œ First Mover Advantage

**Moat 2: í•™ìƒ í–‰ë™ ë°ì´í„° ì¶•ì  (ë°ì´í„°)**
- ë§¤ ë¶„ì„ë§ˆë‹¤ ì¶•ì : ì‘í’ˆ ì´ë¯¸ì§€ + ë©”íŠ¸ë¦­ + fixScope + ì„±ì¥ ê¶¤ì 
- ë²¡í„° DB êµ¬ì¶• (1408-dim embedding)
- ì‹œê°„ì´ ì§€ë‚ ìˆ˜ë¡ ì˜ˆì¸¡ ì •í™•ë„ â†‘:
  - Y1: 70% (ì´ˆê¸°, ì†Œê·œëª¨ ë°ì´í„°)
  - Y2: 80% (MAU 25,000, ì¤‘ê°„ ê·œëª¨)
  - Y3: 85%+ (MAU 100,000, ëŒ€ê·œëª¨)
- **ë„¤íŠ¸ì›Œí¬ íš¨ê³¼**: ì‚¬ìš©ì â†‘ â†’ ë°ì´í„° â†‘ â†’ ì •í™•ë„ â†‘ â†’ ì‹ ê·œ ì‚¬ìš©ì â†‘

**Moat 3: ì…ì‹œí•™ì› íŒŒíŠ¸ë„ˆì‹­ (B2B2C)**
- í•™ì› ê°•ì‚¬ìš© API ì œê³µ â†’ í•™ìƒ ìì—° ìœ ì…
- Revenue Share (20%) â†’ í•™ì›ê³¼ Win-Win
- í•™ì›-í•™ìƒ ì–‘ìª½ Lock-in íš¨ê³¼
- **Sticky**: í•™ìƒì´ í•™ì›ê³¼ DesignMate ë™ì‹œ ì‚¬ìš© â†’ ì´íƒˆë¥  â†“

**Moat 4: dysapp ê¸°ìˆ  ìì‚° (ê¸°ìˆ ì )**
- fixScope ë¡œì§ (StructureRebuild vs DetailTuning)
- 3-Layer ë””ìì¸ í‰ê°€ í”„ë ˆì„ì›Œí¬
- ì´ë¯¸ ê²€ì¦ëœ í”„ë¡¬í”„íŒ… ì „ëµ
- **Time to Market**: dysapp ì´ì‹ â†’ ê°œë°œ ì‹œê°„ 30% ë‹¨ì¶•

### 7.3 Competitive Landscape

**ì§ì ‘ ê²½ìŸì‚¬ (Direct)**
